[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The high CPU time reported for the main thread [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m26[0m[39m seconds of CPU time[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **CellFormatter.format**: Examine line [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m and surrounding code for loops, [0m     [2m                [0m
